Usage:  [option] <argument>

Options:
    -h, --help                   Print program usage message
    -t, --title <text>           Title text
    -b, --body <text>            Body text
    -w, --width <size>           Width size
    -h, --height <size>          Height size
    -x, --xpos <position>        Location in the x-direction to move
    -y, --ypos <position>        Location in the y-direction to move
    --time <seconds>             Amount of time (in seconds) to display
    -o, --opacity <value>        Opacity (0 <= value <= 1)
    -m, --margin <value>         Box margins(0 < value)
    -f, --font <font>            Text font
    -ts, --title-size <size>     Size of text for the title
    -bs, --body-size <size>      Size of text for the body
    -bg, --background <color>    Color of the notification bubble
    -fg, --foreground <color>    Color of the text

Arguments:
    <text>                       Text to display
    <size>                       Size of the notification bubble
    <position>                   X-Y position of the notitification bubble
    <value>                      An integer or double value
    <font>                       Text font
    <size>                       Text size
    <color>                      Hexadecimal color
